 Just keep in mind one thing
 voter ycard ban jane se koi voter nahin ho jaataa he
 The job of the voter is to choose the candidate and not the government
 mujhe pataa he ki aap abhi skool se nikle hai, college main gaye hai
 During this time, you have spent a good amount of time from school to coaching
 mal se lekar pub main bhi guzara he
 There are also passes in the playgrounds
 is umr main yahi sab hota he
 You are looking for yourself and people in the family are pushing towards someone else
 yahi hota he jab aap matadaata banakar maidan main aate hai
 Everyone will keep turning you on their side
 aapako is baar matadaata bananaa he
 Do not think that you turned 18 and became a voter
 is tarah kaa matadaata kisi kaam kaa nahin hota he

 There are many things that you should do before reaching the polling station
 ye koi nahin batayega

 uske liye aap maatr ek number hai

 65 se badhkar 67 fisadi matdaan ho gaya

 matlab usee tarah se jhooth bolegaa or khud ko kisi cinemai nayak kii tarah pesh karegaa
 He will create such a web of rumors and myths that you will get caught in it on the very first day
 aapse pehle bhi log funs chuke hai or aaj tak fanse hue hai

 matadaata bananaa pratishat main gina janaa nahin hota he
 a good voter is one who works hard before voting
 tarkon kaa istemaal karata he, tarah-tarah kii pahchaan ke naam par bhadakaai gai bhavukta main nahin bahata he
 The leader will try to reach you through different identity or emotional issues

 He will not have any morality of his own, but he will give moral education in conversation
 aise netaaon se bachie jo niti kii baat kam kare or netaa-netaa zyaada kare

 aap 18 saal ke ho chuke yuvaaon ke bandal maatr nahin hai
 The sly leader will try to surround you like a bundle, but you get yourself out of the bundle
 kisi bhi sarkaar kaa moolyankan aap is aadhaar par kiijie ki media kitna swatantra he

 vaikalpik awaazon or virodh ke swar ko kitni jagah milti he or gungan ko kitni
 You must do this while reading newspapers and watching news channels
 dhyaan rahe, akhbaar kareedne se akhbaar padhanaa nahin aa jaataa he

 yahi kaam aap tivi ke saath karen
 Calculate what he is showing and what he is not showing
 kya nahin dikhaa rahaa he jab aap isaki ginati karenge to pataa chalegaa ki news channel kis tarah loktantr ko kamazor kar rahe hai
 Do not take information from any one newspaper or one channel
 tarah tarah ke madhyamon kaa istamaal karen or soochnaaon kii prastuti ko lekar apana vishleshan khud karen

 desh bhar ke lakhon yuva sarkari bhartee board se pareshaan hai
 The media never puts their troubles on the front page
 aapaki bhi nahin chhaapega

 agar koi sarkaar kamazor tabake kii parvaah nahin sunati he to aap use kaise apana mat de sakate hai

 Pakistan said it used the JF 17 Thunder fighter aircraft in the operation which it has developed jointly with China
 pakistani sena ke pravaktaa major general asif gafoor ne 14 farvari ko pulavama aatankwaadi hamale ke baad bhartiya vayusena ke saath hawaii sangharsh kaa ullekh karte hue kaha ki bhartiya ladaaku vimaanon ne 26 farvari ko pakistani hawaii seemaa kaa ulanghan kiya or bam giraaye lekin isamen koi hataahat nahin hua or na hi aadharbhoot dhaanche ko koi nuksaan hi hua
 Pakistani terrorist organization Jaishe Mohammad claimed responsibility for the terrorist attack on 14 February in Pulwama targeting the CRPF convoy
 bhartiya vayusena dwaara balakot main jaishe mohammad thikaane par hawaii hamalon kaa jawaab dene ke pakistan ke prayaas ke ek din baad bhartiya sashastr balon ne epa 16 dwaara daagi gai em 120 emram (advanced medium range air tu air missile) ke hisse dikhaaye the jo ki bhartiya kshetra main gire the
 India also said that the electronic signature recorded by the Indian radar confirms the use of F16 by Pakistan
 america videsh mantralay ne ghoshnaa kii ki vah bharat ke khilaaf america nirmit epa16 vimaanon ke sambhavit istemaal ke bare main pakistan se or soochna maang rahaa he
 The use of F16 in this way is a violation of the agreement in this regard
 gafoor ne roosi samvaad samiti sputanik international se kaha ki jis vimaan ne lakshyon ke saath sangharsh kiya vah jeef17 tha

 kyonki us samay hamaari puri vayusena alert par thi
